It's simple to find new brands to work with, apply for their programs and then create affiliate links. I love the dashboard that gives me a good overview of my account's status. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I wish that they had a browser plugin that could be used to create affilliate links directly from shop websites like some other programs have. class="expanded-review-5332978 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Impact helps Sometimes I don't bother. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5309422 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I can't recall any problems Impact has helped me solve. We were told that by using their system we could increase our customer accounts because it would allow influencers to recommend our services. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The quality of the influencers I am attracting. Their program is very easy to learn and implement.
